cap_modifier = {
	# clr_modifers = {
	# 	modifier = $modifier$
	# }
	# set_variable = {
	# 	which = $modifier$
	# 	value = 0
	# }
	export_to_variable = {
		variable_name = $modifier$
		value = modifier:$modifier$
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		which = $modifier$
		value = -1
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = cap_$modifier$
		value = $cap$
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = $modifier$
				which = cap_$modifier$
			}
		}

		subtract_variable = {
			which = $modifier$
			which = cap_$modifier$
		}

		choice_modifier = {
			modifiers = $modifier$
		}
	}

}
